    SELECT [o].[Id], [o].[OrderDate], [o].[CustomerId], COALESCE(SUM(CAST([o0].[Quantity] AS decimal(10,2)) * [o0].[Price]), 0.0) AS [c]
    FROM [Orders] AS [o]
    INNER JOIN [OrderDetails] AS [o0] ON [o].[Id] = [o0].[OrderId]
    INNER JOIN [Medicines] AS [m] ON [o0].[MedicineId] = [m].[Id]
    GROUP BY [o].[Id], [o].[CustomerId], [o].[OrderDate], [o].[CustomerId]
) AS [s]

SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[OrderDate], [s].[CustomerId], [s0].[MedicineName], [s0].[Quantity], [s0].[Price], [s0].[Total], [s0].[Id], [s0].[Id0], [s0].[Id1], [s].[c]
FROM (
    SELECT [o].[Id], [o].[OrderDate], [o].[CustomerId], COALESCE(SUM(CAST([o0].[Quantity] AS decimal(10,2)) * [o0].[Price]), 0.0) AS [c]
    FROM [Orders] AS [o]
    INNER JOIN [OrderDetails] AS [o0] ON [o].[Id] = [o0].[OrderId]
    INNER JOIN [Medicines] AS [m] ON [o0].[MedicineId] = [m].[Id]
    GROUP BY [o].[Id], [o].[CustomerId], [o].[OrderDate], [o].[CustomerId]
) AS [s]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [m0].[Name] AS [MedicineName], [o2].[Quantity], [o2].[Price], CAST([o2].[Quantity] AS decimal(10,2)) * [o2].[Price] AS [Total], [o1].[Id], [o2].[Id] AS [Id0], [m0].[Id] AS [Id1], [o1].[CustomerId], [o1].[OrderDate]
    FROM [Orders] AS [o1]
    INNER JOIN [OrderDetails] AS [o2] ON [o1].[Id] = [o2].[OrderId]
